<Time>1572024124411</Time><Rate>1< /Rate><Text>I hired a Wrench tech to do a simple oil change in May before I moved across the country from GA to CA. Halfway through the road trip in CO, my check engine light came on and the car lost a vast amount of power (error code = drivetrain malfunction). After driving drastically below the speed limit for the remainder of the trip, I took my car to a BMW dealership in CA where they shared some really trouble diagnostics. The results "shocked" the BMW techs; the oil hadn't been changed "in a very very long time", resulting in a "crunched together" filter - driven by using aftermarket filters. They also discovered significant sludge build up. In everyday jargon, my engine was effectively destroyed.

When I mentioned that I'd had my oil changed by a Wrench tech in May, I received this response from the BMW techs: "Two things may have happened: Either someone has changed the oil but not the filter for the oil several times, or someone said he changed the oil but actually just reset the light without doing any work."

I shared this with Wrench on September 24th via email and included photos of the engine + oil filter, a written diagnostic from certified BMW techs and receipts detailing the work allegedly done by the Wrench tech in May. I have yet to receive an email back from Wrench, a month later. I'd hoped to resolve the issue offline, without need for public commentary, but I did not receive a response to my email.

<Time>1615310476128</Time>< Text>
I had a great experience at this location. It was my 1st time here and it did not disappoint. I have never been to a ShareTea before and was pleasantly surprise with the many options of drink. They had milk-teas, smoothies, and even mojitos. The mojitos are virgin, they just make it have a mojito "flavoring."

One of my favorite things about this place is that they have milk alternatives. I have lactose intolerance and I am so glad that I can get almond/soy milk in my boba instead of suffering from a post-boba stomach-ache. I ordered a Wintermelon Milk Tea with boba, herb jelly, and almond milk. I got light ice and 30% sweetness. It was one of the best Wintermelon drink that I have tasted, and I will go back for sure!

The service was friendly and they had great COVID-19 precautions. They had the glass and only allowing 5 people inside at once. After ordering the drink, you have to wait outside to wait for your number to be called. If you do not like that, just order online for pick-up.< /Text>

<pictures>None</pictures><time>1616862862050<//time>< review>
Tacos are really great. Reasonably priced and stuffed with meat. I'm usually a pretty big eater and found that three were enough for dinner. They have several meat options beyond just steak, chicken, carnitas. The al pastor was very good, maybe could be a little juicier and spicier. The carnitas was excellent, crispy and had some additional seasoning that I haven't encountered on carnitas before. They make their own horchata--it's not overly sweet or heavy like you often trying. Great place to sit outside and enjoy a beer in nice weather.</review>

<time>1460707470275<//time>< Rating>
5<//Rating>
<Text>Best burrito place in Healdsburg, probably in Sonoma County! Almost everything they make is traditionally hand made from family recipes passed down from the old generation, but twisted just enough to fit "California Mexican" food while maintaining authenticity (but it's not a yuppie place at all).  Try the chicken fajita burrito. It's awesome! They also have some great veggie options, like the Burrito Guadalajara, which is not billed as vegan, but is simply delicious food that just HAPPENS to be vegan  (probably... I mean, at least it says on the menu it has no dairy or meat). I'm not a vegan, but I do appreciate scrumptious, healthy food...  and the Guadalajara burrito delivers!  The main thing that sets it apart is that this burrito has some nice veggies in it instead of just being a "regular burrito" with no meat (like most veggie burritos), so it's extra good!! Prices are still reasonable (especially for Healdsburg), staff is friendly, food comes out fast, place is clean, has a nice mural on one wall.  I highly recommend it, especially for burritos, but also for the rest of their food!<//Text><pictures>None< /pictures>< Response>
None< /Response>

<rate>5<//rate>< Review>
As an El Monte resident, I cannot believe I had not discovered this place before!

The service is adorable! It's family-oriented and has a very homely feeling. If you are a regular, the staff will recognize you and will converse with you about how you're doing, what you're up to, etc.

The food is great for an affordable price. It's a great deal deal here. Probably one of the best breakfast spots in El Monte.

If you're looking for a mom-and-pop joint in this area, I highly recommend this spot!<//Review>

<Date>1460754359999</Date><rate>5<//rate><Text>Great hole in the wall breakfast joint. I would say skip Denny's or Ihop and grab some food that Isn't chucked out of the kitchen like some soulless factory. If you're around Saturday or Sunday their menudo is great. A small plate is just under $6 and it was enough and delicious. Next, try their country fried steak with a side of tater tots and a biscuit and gravy. I really don't care for biscuits but I love to dip my tater tots in the gravy and its gooood with 4 o's.  If your just in the mood for some traditional eggs, sausage, bacon, hash-brown, and pancakes then this place  won't let you down. Finally just wanted to add that its one of those places that has been there forever, or at least it seems like that. You'll see the walls covered in pictures of El Monte from the early 1900's. < Review>
I've been using Wave for about 9 months now.  I live alone (with a big dog) in a moderately sized 2 bedroom apartment and I'm a very neat person, so I only have them come once a month to frankly do the things I don't want to do, like clean the showers and my stove.  They do a great job and the women who have come into my home couldn't have been nicer or more friendly to my dog (which is very important to me).

Speaking of showers, it's often the little things that define quality of service.  This week the woman who cleaned my place got my glass shower door cleaner than I've ever been able to get it.  It's long suffered from years and years of hard water and soap deposits.  Not even CLR could get it all clean.  But after this week's cleaning it is completely clear. I don't know what she used, but it was amazing.

It's also often how a company handles service issues that defines quality of service.  The one time I contacted the office about something the cleaner missed (a floor left wet after being cleaned), they got back to me almost immediately and offered to send someone to fix the situation right away.</Review>

I've been wanting to have periodic maid service for some time, however, my significant other is not very trusting after she had some jewelry boosted by some movers.  I convinced her that we'd go with a company that is insured and I'd leave work early to be at the home while the cleaning occurred. I opened the door and the maid (Marisol?) got right to work, attacking the master bath first.
